      <h1 class="page-title">Search Products that Meet the Safer Choice Standard</h1>
      <!--googleoff: all-->
    
            
    
    <!--googleon: all-->
    
  
    

  <div class="row row-a cols-1">          <div class="col">      
<div class="panel-pane pane-fieldable-panels-pane pane-vid-134477 pane-bundle-fieldable-panels-pane pane-fpid-2809">

  
  
  
  
  
  <div class="pane-content">
    <p><a class="exit-disclaimer" href="https://espanol.epa.gov/saferchoice/busque-productos-que-cumplan-con-la-norma-safer-choice" id="spanish" title="haga clic aquí para ver el contenido en español">en español</a></p>

<p>Looking for safer cleaning and other products? Use the search box below to find products that meet the Safer Choice Standard.</p>

	jQuery('#selType').css('margin-top','6px');
  
    //override sorting arrows provided in datatables, using standard epa table arrows
	var base64StringSorting = "PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIGhlaWdodD0iMTAuMDE0OTciIHdpZHRoPSI4LjAwMDA0MSIgdmVyc2lvbj0iMS4xIiB4bWxuczpkYz0iaHR0cDovL3B1cmwub3JnL2RjL2VsZW1lbnRzLzEuMS8iPg0KPGcgZmlsbD0iIzE1MTUxNSIgdHJhbnNmb3JtPSJ0cmFuc2xhdGUoMTM5LjQ0MzY2LC0yMzcuMTM2NTcpIj4NCjxwYXRoIHRyYW5zZm9ybT0ibWF0cml4KDAuMjg1NzI1NjgsMCwwLDAuMTY0OTYzOCwtMTEwLjAxNDA3LDIzNi40NjI3MikiIGQ9Ik0tNzUuMDAwNTU4LDI4LjMzMjU4Mi04OSwyOC4zMzI1ODFoLTEzLjk5OTQ0bDYuOTk5NzItMTIuMTIzODcxLDYuOTk5NzItMTIuMTIzODczLDYuOTk5NzIsMTIuMTIzODczeiIvPg0KPHBhdGggdHJhbnNmb3JtPSJtYXRyaXgoLTAuMjg1NzI1NjgsMCwwLC0wLjE2NDk2MzgsLTE2MC44NzMyLDI0Ny44MjUzOSkiIGQ9Ik0tNzUuMDAwNTU4LDI4LjMzMjU4Mi04OSwyOC4zMzI1ODFoLTEzLjk5OTQ0bDYuOTk5NzItMTIuMTIzODcxLDYuOTk5NzItMTIuMTIzODczLDYuOTk5NzIsMTIuMTIzODczeiIvPg0KPC9nPg0KPC9zdmc+";

    var sortEvent = function ( type ) { 
        jQuery('table.dataTable thead .sorting').css("background-image", "url('data:image/svg+xml;base64," + base64StringSorting + "')");  
		jQuery('table.dataTable thead .sorting_asc').css("background-image", "url('data:image/svg+xml;base64," + base64StringSortingUp + "')");
		jQuery('table.dataTable thead .sorting_desc').css("background-image", "url('data:image/svg+xml;base64," + base64StringSortingDown + "')");
    }
	
    var oTable =  jQuery("#tblData")
	.on( 'order.dt',  function () { sortEvent( 'Order' ); } )
	.DataTable({
	     "order": [3,'asc'],
		 "pageLength": 25,
		"dom": '<"top"lp<"clear">>rt<"bottom"ip<"clear">>',
		data: dataSet,
		"columns": [
			  { data: "Name" }
			, { data: "Partner" }
			, { data: "sector" }
			, { data: "sectorType" }
			, { data: "releases" }
			, { data: "fragrance" }
			, { data: "biobased" }
		],
		"columnDefs": [
			  { "targets": [4,5,6], "visible": false }   // hides the searchable but not displayed columns, i.e. header-ids: releases, fragrance, biobased
			, { "targets": [0],							 // template for first column to link to pop-up
			    "width": "45%",
			    "render": function( data, type, row ) {
						return "<a class='colorbox-inline' href='#"+row.Id+"'>" + row.Name + "</a>";
					} 
			  }
		]
	 });

	 jQuery('#tblData tbody').on( 'click', 'a.colorbox-inline', function () {
		var data = oTable.row( jQuery(this).parents('tr') ).data();
		var contentHTML = 
		  '<p><b>'+data.Name+'</b>'
		+ '<br />UPC(s): '+(data.UPCs ? data.UPCs : 'N/A' )
		+ (data.fragrance ? '<br/>Fragrance-Free' : '')
		+ (data.releases ? '<br />Acceptable for outdoor use' : '' ) // Or 'Has outdoor uses' (TBD)
		//+ (data.biobased ? '<br />Also USDA Certified Biobased' : '' )
		+ '<br /><a class="search" href="http://www.google.com/search?q='+encodeURIComponent(data.Name)+'+'+encodeURIComponent(data.Partner)+'" target="_blank">Search Product Availability</a>'
		+ '</p>	<p>	<b>Partner Information</b>'
		+ '<br />Company Name: '+data.Partner
		+ '<br />Safer Choice Partner Since: ' + data.PartnerSince 
		+ '<br /></p>'
		
		jQuery.colorbox({html:contentHTML, width:"50%"});
     } );
	 
	 jQuery('#tblData_length').css('margin-top','13px');
     jQuery('#tblData_paginate').css('margin-bottom','10px');
	 jQuery('.dataTables_filter').css('display','none');

	 jQuery('table.dataTable thead .sorting').css("background-image", "url('data:image/svg+xml;base64," + base64StringSorting + "')");
	 jQuery('table.dataTable thead .sorting_asc').css("background-image", "url('data:image/svg+xml;base64," + base64StringSortingUp + "')");
	 jQuery('table.dataTable thead .sorting_desc').css("background-image", "url('data:image/svg+xml;base64," + base64StringSortingDown + "')");
	 
    //process incoming links that include search filters such as "type=Deicers" in url
	if (window.location.hash) {
		  var hash = decodeURI(location.hash.substring(1, location.hash.length)); 
		  var params = hash.split(/[&]+/); 

		  var paramArray = [];
		  
		  for (var i=0;i<params.length;i++) {
				var pairs = [];
				pairs = params[i].split('=');
				paramArray.push(pairs);
		  }

		  for (var j=0;j<paramArray.length;j++) {
				
			if (paramArray[j][0] == 'type') {
				jQuery('#selType').val(paramArray[j][1]);
				oTable.columns( [3] ).search( paramArray[j][1]==='all' ? '' : paramArray[j][1] ,true,true,false).draw();
			}
			else if (paramArray[j][0] == 'sector') {
				jQuery('#selSector').val(paramArray[j][1]);
				oTable.columns( [2] ).search( paramArray[j][1]==='all' ? '' : paramArray[j][1] ).draw();
			}
			else if (paramArray[j][0] == 'fragrance') {
				jQuery('#selSector').val(paramArray[j][1]);
				oTable.columns( [5] ).search( paramArray[j][1]==='all' ? '' : paramArray[j][1] ).draw();
			}
			else if (paramArray[j][0] == 'releases') {
				jQuery('#selSector').val(paramArray[j][1]);
				oTable.columns( [4] ).search( paramArray[j][1]==='all' ? '' : paramArray[j][1] ).draw();
			}

			else if (paramArray[j][0] == 'search') {
				oTable.search( paramArray[j][1], false, false).draw(); 
			}
		  }
		  jQuery(document).scrollTop(jQuery('#tblData').offset().top);
	}

    //search filter controls tied to options in green box
	jQuery('#searchProduct').keyup(function() {
	    var selectedValue = jQuery(this).val();
		oTable.search( selectedValue, false, false).draw(); 
	});
	jQuery( "#selType" ).change(function() {
		var selectedValue = jQuery(this).val(); 
		oTable.columns( [3] ).search( selectedValue==='all' ? '' : selectedValue,true,true,false ).draw();
	});
	jQuery( "#selSector" ).change(function() {
		var selectedValue = jQuery(this).val();
		oTable.columns( [2] ).search( selectedValue==='all' ? '' : selectedValue ).draw();
	});
    jQuery('#selReleases').on('click',function(){
        var checked = jQuery('#selReleases').is(':checked')
		oTable.columns( [4] ).search( checked ? 'Yes' : '' ).draw();
    });		
    jQuery('#selFragrance').on('click',function(){
        var checked = jQuery('#selFragrance').is(':checked')
		oTable.columns( [5] ).search( checked ? 'Yes' : '' ).draw();
    });	
    jQuery('#selAudit').on('click',function(){
        var checked = jQuery('#selAudit').is(':checked')
		oTable.columns( [6] ).search( checked ? 'Yes' : '' ).draw();
    });	
});
